<br />
Last year I sampled this a few times and got huge fake strawberry and jam. Today (very cool spring morning) it’s more of a blurred berry almost a jus with sharp tannic edges and softly sweet. No plastic. <br />
<br />
Plenty of spicy cinnamon and patchouli up front with a clean musk and wood base. Feels like leather is appearing (warm dark brown leather that has been heated by a body and is giving that vibe of comfort). No Animalic edges. <br />
<br />
I’m surprised at how much I’m liking it. The odd spike of a fruit that’s sharp (like the mango does in GOF) to offset the spicy caramel sweetness. <br />
<br />
Amazing how much the sample, my nose or both can change over time. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1878218">Scratch &amp; Sniff</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-06">09/06/24 23:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There is no venom being spat here, merely a harmless spray of fruit.<br />
<br />
And let's be honest with each other, you're not really buying this for the fragrance itself.  Nay, you're purchasing this for the online hype and the stunning bottle.  Go on, I won't judge you, the bottle *is* gorgeous.<br />
<br />
But please don't act like this scent is anything more sophisticated than a fruity cocktail of frozen and pre-packaged strawberries and raspberries carelessly dropped into a blender by a disgruntled mall worker at Jamba Juice.  I don't dislike this scent, but paying $230.00 for it would be...questionable.  Supposedly, there are notes of leather that appear at some point, but I've worn this unambitious scent for an entire day and it's been completely linear from beginning through to end.<br />
<br />
Of all the scents I've tried from Stéphane Humbert Lucas 777's La Serpent Collection, the only one that is truly worth your time and money is Mortal Skin.<br />
<br />
In five words or less: Synthetic strawberries.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="2274282"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=2274282#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2271671" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="2168647"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=2168647#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2164092" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2164092" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="sntiago"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2047146"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2047146.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="sntiago" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Lattafa-Perfumes/Ajayeb-Dubai-Portrait-84222.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.84222.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Ajayeb Dubai Portrait"title="Ajayeb Dubai Portrait"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2164092ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2164092" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2047146">sntiago</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-22">05/22/24 07:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Opens with a very sharp and sour strawberry. It dries down to a fruity sweet, kind of powdery strawberry. I do no get much of a leather scent - at least no "in your face" leather. More of like a subtle suede blended into the fruits. It's not much more exciting than any strawberry kids shampoo at the start - but it is a very nice strawberry scent. As it develops it gets less sweet, with a bit of spice, mostly from the patchouli. <br />
Compared to stuff like Burberry Her, where the "strawberry" is screechy and synthetic and unpleasant - this one actually wears nicely. You have to like fruits to wear this. <br />
The fruitiness stays through the wear but much much more subdued than in the opening and it's kind of basic and unassuming. I'm not really a fruity scents kind of person and wish the leather was stronger (as it's more woodsy than leathery). <br />
Having one Sand dance on one arm and Venom Incarnat on the other, Sand dance trumps it in terms of projection by a mile. <br />
<br />
<br />
In conclusion: love the strong berry opening, but the dry down kind of disappointed. <br />
Safe blind buy for berry lovers.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="2164092"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=2164092#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2161141" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2161141" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Dbrummag"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2086854"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Dbrummag" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2161141ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2161141" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2086854">Dbrummag</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-19">05/19/24 11:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>You can really tell the difference on this fragrance between reviewers that tested on skin over a long period of time and those that just wrote a review based on the opening.<br />
<br />
It is true that this one opens very sweet with a strawberry note. My first thought was wow this smells quite cheap, kind of like a $20 body mist from some teen clothing store. I didn’t like it and said in my mind, well that’s that. I came back and put my nose on it a bit later … this can’t be the same fragrance … I must have sleep walked over and sprayed something else on my wrist. <br />
<br />
  I’ve never experienced a perfume change to a larger degree than this one. One of the major differences to me of a good niche fragrance and designer is niche perfumery going through 2-3 transitions and new notes emerging. Most accomplish that by the opening being very short lived followed by a middle that comprises most of the performance and then a skin scent of base notes. Here, the sweet strawberry opening stays around longer, 1-2 hours, but by hours 2-4  you get this smoked leather that’s coming from the combination of patchouli, tonka bean, and leather but smoothed by the vanilla with hints of woods. On my skin, the strawberry is completely gone. The fragrance has done a complete 180. It’s not a mixing of notes, there is no thread of DNA recognizable from the opening to the end … it’s an entirely different scent. It’s remarkably well blended master perfumery to accomplish this and also to have it be consistent between wears. <br />
<br />
I still don’t like the opening, I do enjoy the dry down although it’s not that unique. I love the overall scent though because it’s like a magic trick in a bottle that very few others have managed to pull off.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="2161141"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=2161141#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2159950" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1422647">Vlad the Impala</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-18">05/18/24 07:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>THE STRAWBERRY TEST 🍓<br />

I don't get obsessed often (last time I did it was BR540 about 5 years ago) but this is my newest love love love.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1935880"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1935880#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1924110" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; If anyone reading this has tried AA and also detects a strawberry note imagine that amped up and the vanilla toned down so the leather can shine through and now you’re getting in to venom incarnat territory.<br />
<br />
When you first spray, your nose will be hit with a super feminine strawberry that smells like the strawberry lip balms you used to get in the early 2000’s but then give it a few seconds for it to develop on your skin and then the magic happens. Next you get the leather and the fragrance transforms from a girly fruity fragrance to something very unique with a lot of character and depth. The contrast of something nostalgic, girly and youthful against this smoky dark leathery vanilla is just so unique and the way they’ve blended the notes together is just magic. <br />
 <br />
Kind of smells like you’re wearing a sexy leather jacket smoking strawberry flavoured shisha - but in the best way possible!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1889308"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1889308#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1879979" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1879979" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RGH01"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1331188.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="RGH01" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1879979ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1879979" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188">RGH01</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-07-16">07/16/23 07:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Venom Incarnat is a very interesting and unique perfume, but to me goes in the wrong direction. It opens instantly with an intensely sweet strawberry and raspberry combination, with a juicy blackberry and thick caramel supporting this. <br />
<br />
There’s a gentle spiciness from the cinnamon, while the base is comprised of a smooth and thick leather and vanilla combo. It’s not particularly unpleasant and I can see they were really trying to push the boat out by utilising such a unique set of notes; however, a natural strawberry does not exist, and so by making it the main note of the fragrance you’re left with an extremely synthetic and low quality fruitiness that’s more reminiscent of strawberry flavoured medicine than a natural strawberry.<br />
<br />
Unfortunately to me this fragrance smells very plasticky and does not live up to the high quality ingredients that I know this house uses in its other releases. I would not recommend this perfume unless you really want to smell like fake strawberries.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1879979"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1879979#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1879055" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Big like!<br />
<br />
Also I'm getting some le labo baie 19 vibes in the air.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1879055"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1879055#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1878044" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/614231">jassca99</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-06-03">06/03/23 13:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It is really difficult to avoid synthetic car freshener with strawberry notes, which is what I get in the very opening going straight to my head. It’s saved because it dies down quickly to a clean leather appearing immediately with the strawberry and another berry muddled in the background. Similarities with Xerjoff La Capitale except La Capitale has a brighter strawberry, sharper leather, incense, and less caramel which forces me to layer with a vanilla/caramel fragrance to balance the sharpness. La Venom is sweeter but never sticky because the caramel hands the baton to the tonka, who is the leader in the dry-down, while the leather still wraps around the caramel and straw/berries buffing any jagged edges that comes with the fruit. I’m surprised this isn’t tart as wild strawberries are listed, but I’m not mad at it. This is very well blended and gets better the longer you wear. Projection is good. Longevity as well.<br />
<br />
The Byron Parfums Mula Mulas, Xerjoff La Capitale and SHL Venom Incarnate are similar and all upwards $200, so no choice is really a bad one if you like this profile (as I stated on my Mula Mula review).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1836953" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Ninamariah"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1588494"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1588494.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Ninamariah" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Roja-Dove/Isola-Sol-91214.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.91214.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Isola Sol"title="Isola Sol"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1836953ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1836953" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1588494">Ninamariah</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-05-19">05/19/23 08:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Female leaning<br />
<br />
I like to wear this scent during the summertime and I fell in love with two years ago while testing it in hot Italy weather.<br />
<br />
How is this beauty? It opens up with a juicy Strawberry and Wild Strawberry notes and I love it. It’s quite sweet since there is a caramel note as well but woody and leather notes push the sweetness down after the dry down. I think this is so special for me since wild strawberry brings me back to my childhood memories when picking up those and when stringing them into the hay. I don’t get any Raspberries but I think it blends into Strawberries. This is not typical light girly Strawberry scent, it’s unique like all SHL:s creations. There is all the time certain kind of depth in the background. Juice vibe turns into soft Vanilla and Tonka but I can smell the hint of the Strawberry until the end.<br />
<br />
During the cold days this is not so beautiful but it’s just my opinion. Anyway this is really different in cold than in really hot so I recommend to test how it differs in your skin. All that synthetic feeling disappears in hot and all the notes are blending better. The hotter the better. Strawberry and caramel melt on my skin into very intoxicating sweet aroma. In wintertime I'm wondering why I even have this perfume and when the summer arrives I remember why I fell in love with this scent.<br />
<br />
I have noticed that some people compare this to La Capitale by Xerjoff and even think that’s this is redundant if you already have La Capitale but imo there is nothing same how these two perform. There is many same notes in those two and it looks like a same but especially Strawberry note is very different in those. La Capitale is really delicate compared to this. This has more character and a deeper woody touch. I think there is different occasions to wear those.<br />
<br />
Thank you for reading and I would appreciate a lot if you want to follow me on IG: @ninamariah_perfumes</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1836953"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1836953#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1833381" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; May 2023<br />
<br />
Wow, they main note according to votes is wild strawberry??!! It is either people want to believe it, or they have never smelled wild strawberry in their life. Seriously, wild strawberry grows in my moms garden and this perfume smells nothing like it. It does not smells like strawberry or raspberry as well. Or at least it does smell of something that we call strawberry or raspberry note in perfumery - a very synthetic one. But to me this fragrance is all about leather with addition of plastic "berry note", which i would say more of a blackberry, than all other red berries listed above. Leather note is actually very well done, but the side blackberry note is ruining it for me. I could only bear half an hour or even less and had to wash it off, so off-puting it was. <br />
So, apart of the beautiful bottle it is not a great fragrance, tbh. At least it is very weird one, and not enjoyable (for me at least). I do not know where it wants to belong? It does not fit well with leathery fragrances, yet too platicky and synthetis for summer berry fragrances. It is a big confusion for me. A hard pass.<br />
P.S. It actually smells something like Valentino´s "Valentina Pink", but without the strong leathery note.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1833381"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1833381#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1825777" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
It's not a bad fragrance, smells boujie for sure... In my opinion, it leans a bit feminine, but not too much.<br />
<br />
I don't get the note listing here since the note I get the most is licorice and it's not listed. I don't get the the rasberry nor the blackberry notes, the strawberry is soft and synthetic. It smells medicinal, like a herbal store and a bit like cough syrup in a strange luxurious way. This is the type of scent that gives me headaches, but strangely, this one doesn't.<br />
It think it would smell pleasant on someone else, I would enjoy getting whiffs in the air of this scent, but just not on me, because the scent tires me. Luckily, it has a very moderate longevity, after 4 hours I couldn't find any aroma on my wrist. But for 3 hours, the sillage is strong.<br />
<br />
I expected a different scent from the notes, the color of the bottle and the name of the perfume, but it's an elegant scent. Not bad. A bit pricey though. I don't recommend due to longevity. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1563263">PerfumePixie87</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-03-30">03/30/23 12:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A conventionally sexy female offering. I’m sure a vast majority of heterosexual men would love to smell this on a woman. A sweet caramel gourmand with touches of leather and red berries. The most surprising thing about Venom Incarnat is that the realistic strawberry note is pervasive and sticks around until the dry down. This is the subversive scent of glamorous vampy eye make up plus leather biker jacket but finished off with strawberry chapstick. Strawberry is a tricky note to utilise without making a scent smell synthetic or lean juvenile. In this realm of tooth achingly sweet, flirty gourmands I prefer Orchidee Rouge by Sora Dora.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1796436"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1796436#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1794720" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I am happy with the scent and the performance. Personally think it reminds me of La Capitale from Xerjoff, if you have that, you don't need this</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1725340"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1725340#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1717925" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1717925" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="nkapped"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1559046"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="nkapped" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1717925ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1717925" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1559046">nkapped</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-12-26">12/26/22 17:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A tale of two strawberries. <br />
<br />
The first strawberry is light and carefree, fresh from a bush, mingling joyously with luscious caramel. She is fruity and juicy, all sunshine and sweetness. There are hints of tart raspberry and blackberry and a light woody backbone runs through, cutting through the saccharine embrace.<br />
 <br />
The second strawberry is a creature of the night, mysterious and veiled. A darkness creeps through as she passes and leather and patchouli begin to coat the berry sweetness. It’s altogether deeper, denser and richer. One picks up touches of spice from the cinnamon while a pale, regal vanilla stands sentinel along the border.<br />
 <br />
Venom Incarnat is locked in a tension between these two very different strawberries. It’s both sweet and moody, light and dark. The fragrance is relatively linear in terms of its development but these contrasts give it lovely texture. I get moderate projection and decent longevity before it sinks into a pillowy bed of berry-tinged vanilla and wood.<br />
 <br />
All the creations from SHL 777 are works of art and one should also take a moment to admire that stunning bottle design with its ruby red crystal eyes and a cap that so perfectly evokes a strawberry, all gilded and gleaming. A nuanced, shape-shifting strawberry that will slowly steal your heart.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1717925"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1717925#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1716692" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Incredible passionate hate lol but also glowing reviews. Polarizing to say the least! For me Venom Incarnat was a nice follow-up to God of Fire which I have to admit is one the best things I’ve ever smelled, and was unlikely to be topped. But VI wasn’t underwhelming in the least, it has a unique lightly spicy cinnamony-strawberry/fruity-leather combo with some nice warmth and sweetness from the caramel, vanilla and tonka. The strawberry top note is unmistakable once you know what it is. It’s not a heavy or cloying fragrance even with its warmth, making it actually quite versatile! It’s truly not a seasonal fragrance in my mind, and that’s an ode to the brilliant composition with such a smooth leather accord that isn’t heavy yet definitely noticeable. I find the fragrance overall very unisex with it utilizing both feminine and masculine elements, but if I had to on the spot I’d say it leans a tad more masculine. This is one where you will be smelling yourself for hours off the sillage, and I am thoroughly enjoying it. Incredible quality and it looks like I am surely becoming a huge fan of SHL.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1653473"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1653473#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1652214" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1633984" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Moeytja"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1224097"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1224097.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Moeytja" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Sublime-Vanille-7024.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.7024.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Sublime Vanille"title="Sublime Vanille"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1633984ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1633984" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1224097">Moeytja</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-08-29">08/29/22 19:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This perfume. I am just… blown. Away.  This is one of the most incredible perfumes i have smelled in my life! Absolute work of art, intoxicating, unique, just stunning.  A dream come true for the niche fanatic i am.  And let me tell you after collecting perfumes for years, it takes something special and different to wow me like this one did.  This is a very unique take on the fruity patchouli genre.<br />
<br />
My rule of thumb for scents, is that they have to be likeable and pleasant. Appealing. Enough w the weird unwearable sht.  I do not feel the need to be a niche head wanna be that need something weird an off putting to call this art and masterpiece.  To me this is a masterpiece on the fruity genre, a sexy iteration of feminity, gourmand,  fall, sexy atmosphere.   This is also right up the alley of gourmand niche lovers like myself.<br />
<br />
The scent: the most gorgeous, sweet, juicy and powdery wild strawberry you’ll ever smell.  I think ppl are calling this synthetic because wild strawberry is a rather unusual scent, with a very particular dna and because its really likeable.  This pretty feminine too eh.  And youthful.  To me its a hyper real wild strawberry.  Nothing about this scent points to simple or cheap scent whatsoever.  If signature scents were still a thing, this would be it for me.<br />
<br />
This a very patchouli forward scent. Yep a fruity patchouli. The patchouli here truly stands out in the best possible way.  Its a minty, foresty and fresh camphoric and herbal type of patchouli, green and natural smelling.  Think of a fresh, green botanical garden while you are eating a wild sweet strawberry bowl.  Or a dark, green forest with wild strawberry bushes all around you. Sooo aromatic, sweet, powdery, rich, herbaceous… juicy.<br />
The leather is very much in the background to ground this scent, barely perceptible and blended to perfection.  You can not pick it out almost. It mostly gives to the scent an animalic, sexy af nuance.  It does ever so slightly remind me too of a strawberry vanilla hookah scent, in the best possible way.<br />
<br />
This is a dream fall scent, i see it more for a cooler weather, on a sexy outfit, something casual but not extremely casual.  For a party, cocktails, dinner.  Movies maybe if on a date.  <br />
<br />
The dna is super unique, i have not smelled a gourmand like this.  Has the slightest similar category as la capitale, but very different scents.  This is sooo yummy, likeable, sweet, juicy, powdery, sexy, unique.  Intoxicating and super attractive with All the complexity and intrigue i want from a Niche house.  A true fruity genre masterpiece that has gotten me totally addicted to this and in love w this house and i want all bottles now.  Stephan Humbert… well done.  10/10 scent. <br />

So when I saw a sample for sale, I jumped on it like a rabid fruit bat 🍓 🦇 <br />
<br />
However…<br />
<br />
That juice….I was so hoping to smell all the notes it claims to have 😔 but alas, I smell no strawberries (or any berries), no cinnamon, and certainly no caramel 😭<br />
I was hoping to have gourmand notes accompanied by a note of smoke or incense and honestly, I am sad to say that all I detect is patchouli (and not the good kind), woods and something sickly sticky sweet but not in a good way…there’s something disturbingly sharp and fake too but I cannot really pinpoint what it is…<br />
I am very disappointed but hey, at least, I did not make the mistake of buying a full bottle blindly so there’s that…<br />
<br />
Burberry Her smells more like strawberries than Venom Incarnat. Though admittedly, Her smells a LOT more on the tart side of strawberries, at least, there is a strong presence of strawberries. <br />
<br />
As for the comparison to La Capitale by Xerjoff, it does not smell ANYTHING similar to Venom Incarnat. I own a full bottle of La Capitale and I am doing a comparison right now; La Capitale is an amber/leather perfume and it is so divinely blended and beautiful. Venom Incarnat has nothing to do with it…<br />
<br />
All in all, I am very glad I obtained a generous sample of Venom Incarnat because I was getting overly obsessed with it (I mean, look at that GORGEOUS BOTTLE)…<br />
I think I will try it again over the Fall/Winter months because who knows? My opinion might change? As for now, this is just a definite no for me even though I am totally lusting after that red gorgeous serpentine bottle 🍓🐍<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1562974" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Mark1996"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1246983"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1246983.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Mark1996" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1562974ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1562974" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1246983">Mark1996</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-13">05/13/22 06:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was a blind buy for me - SHL fragrances are an absolute nightmare to get samples of in the UK and thankfully I really like this one. I've tried quite a few other Strawberry dominant fragrances even the hyped up Mula Mula / La Capitale which I was expecting this to smell similar to with them sharing a lot of notes, I can confirm they go in totally different directions.<br />
<br />
This one has just a hint of sourness to balance the sweetness, making it Unisex appropriate. The strawberry smells the most natural out of any strawberry fragrances i've ever tried and doesn't have that cloying effect that usually happens when this note is dominant. Anyways there is a lot more to this fragrance than just strawberry, its ever morphing.. some of the other notes shine in the back and add a lot of depth and a touch of smokiness. Truly a unique fragrance which I've come to expect from SHL. After wearing this for a few days everybody comments how 'different' this one is to my other fragrances and how they love it.<br />
<br />
Would I Buy: Successful blind buy that I received today, may become an all-time favourite in time.<br />
Recommended: Absolutely. I always recommend sampling (hypocrite in this case lol) but this is fairly safe.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1562974"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1562974#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1556935" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1224097">Moeytja</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-08-29">08/29/22 19:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This perfume. I am just… blown. Away.  This is one of the most incredible perfumes i have smelled in my life! Absolute work of art, intoxicating, unique, just stunning.  A dream come true for the niche fanatic i am.  And let me tell you after collecting perfumes for years, it takes something special and different to wow me like this one did.  This is a very unique take on the fruity patchouli genre.<br />
<br />
My rule of thumb for scents, is that they have to be likeable and pleasant. Appealing. Enough w the weird unwearable sht.  I do not feel the need to be a niche head wanna be that need something weird an off putting to call this art and masterpiece.  To me this is a masterpiece on the fruity genre, a sexy iteration of feminity, gourmand,  fall, sexy atmosphere.   This is also right up the alley of gourmand niche lovers like myself.<br />
<br />
The scent: the most gorgeous, sweet, juicy and powdery wild strawberry you’ll ever smell.  I think ppl are calling this synthetic because wild strawberry is a rather unusual scent, with a very particular dna and because its really likeable.  This pretty feminine too eh.  And youthful.  To me its a hyper real wild strawberry.  Nothing about this scent points to simple or cheap scent whatsoever.  If signature scents were still a thing, this would be it for me.<br />
<br />
This a very patchouli forward scent. Yep a fruity patchouli. The patchouli here truly stands out in the best possible way.  Its a minty, foresty and fresh camphoric and herbal type of patchouli, green and natural smelling.  Think of a fresh, green botanical garden while you are eating a wild sweet strawberry bowl.  Or a dark, green forest with wild strawberry bushes all around you. Sooo aromatic, sweet, powdery, rich, herbaceous… juicy.<br />
The leather is very much in the background to ground this scent, barely perceptible and blended to perfection.  You can not pick it out almost. It mostly gives to the scent an animalic, sexy af nuance.  It does ever so slightly remind me too of a strawberry vanilla hookah scent, in the best possible way.<br />
<br />
This is a dream fall scent, i see it more for a cooler weather, on a sexy outfit, something casual but not extremely casual.  For a party, cocktails, dinner.  Movies maybe if on a date.  <br />
<br />
The dna is super unique, i have not smelled a gourmand like this.  Has the slightest similar category as la capitale, but very different scents.  This is sooo yummy, likeable, sweet, juicy, powdery, sexy, unique.  Intoxicating and super attractive with All the complexity and intrigue i want from a Niche house.  A true fruity genre masterpiece that has gotten me totally addicted to this and in love w this house and i want all bottles now.  Stephan Humbert… well done.  10/10 scent. <br />
Follow me at splendid.scents on insta.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1633984"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1633984#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="72387" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1879979" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RGH01"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1331188.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="RGH01" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1879979ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1879979" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188">RGH01</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-07-16">07/16/23 07:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Venom Incarnat is a very interesting and unique perfume, but to me goes in the wrong direction. It opens instantly with an intensely sweet strawberry and raspberry combination, with a juicy blackberry and thick caramel supporting this. <br />
<br />
There’s a gentle spiciness from the cinnamon, while the base is comprised of a smooth and thick leather and vanilla combo. It’s not particularly unpleasant and I can see they were really trying to push the boat out by utilising such a unique set of notes; however, a natural strawberry does not exist, and so by making it the main note of the fragrance you’re left with an extremely synthetic and low quality fruitiness that’s more reminiscent of strawberry flavoured medicine than a natural strawberry.<br />
<br />
Unfortunately to me this fragrance smells very plasticky and does not live up to the high quality ingredients that I know this house uses in its other releases. I would not recommend this perfume unless you really want to smell like fake strawberries.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72387"comment_id="1879979"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Venom-Incarnat-72387.html?ccid=1879979#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1652214" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
